<span id="freeTextContainer9180228369640565559">This is by far the best book of the series so far. Mare was far less annoying.<br/><br/>I can’t believe Glass sword was a 1 star read for me while this was 4 stars. Who would have thought? I’m glad I continued reading.<br/><br/><b> Things I liked </b><br/>- I love how action-packed this was. Some I saw coming, some I didn’t <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ didn’t see the first Maven assassination attempt by the houses who were loyal to cal  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br/><br/>- The first thing I noticed was that this wasn’t in only Mare’s POV and that made me exc</span>
  <span id="freeText9180228369640565559" style="display:none">This is by far the best book of the series so far. Mare was far less annoying.<br /><br />I can’t believe Glass sword was a 1 star read for me while this was 4 stars. Who would have thought? I’m glad I continued reading.<br /><br /><b> Things I liked </b><br />- I love how action-packed this was. Some I saw coming, some I didn’t <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ didn’t see the first Maven assassination attempt by the houses who were loyal to cal  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />- The first thing I noticed was that this wasn’t in only Mare’s POV and that made me excited because if you’ve been following my reviews and updates of this series, you would know I don’t like her. Ironically, I didn’t really mind her chapters in this. She was aight<br /><br />- Evangeline’s chapters were my favourite. I just love her and her mob-like family. I love how powerful her father is that he doesn't have to look powerful to be feared. I love her and her brother’s relationship, although some things were weird about it <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Her, Elane and Tolly’s arrangement was just uncomfortable  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />- Although Maven is….Maven, he made this book really interesting<br /><br />- LONG LIVE TIBERIAS THE SEVENTH!!!!! I LOVE CAL, I LOVE HOW KIND HE IS, I LOVE HOW HE RATHER SAVE THAN KILL, I LOVE HOW HE NEVER GIVES UP ON PEOPLE, I HATE HOW PEOPLE TREAT HIM, I HATE HOW HE DOESN’T HAVE ANYONE. DID I MENTION THAT I LOVE CAL????? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ why are people, especially the reds so against him being king when he would treat them well?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />- Cal’s grandmother. I love how fearless she is and how loyal she is to her grandson 💕<br /><br /><b>There were a few things I didn’t like </b><br />- I don’t like Cameron. I don’t know why she had a POV. She was so annoying and wasn’t important enough for her own perspective. There were better people I would have loved to have instead of her.<br /><br />- Mare during the epilogue <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Okay she asked cal to choose her but wasn’t willing to choose him and then made him seem like the bad guy. How hypocritical. Cal was born to be king but he was betrayed and exiled. He DESERVES to be king!! Now he’s going to feel guilty and stuff ugh.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Okay, can we have a Cal and Maven POV in the final book?? And no more Cameron, please. <br /><br />Something bad better not happen to Cal in War Storm 😤</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7624256031939621521"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You aren’t alone.” The hope in his eyes cuts deeply. “You have your crown.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439246972ra/15813352.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Why???? That ending killed me!!!! Now I see it! Now I feel it! <i>Anyone can betray anyone</i>!<br/>I'm still #teamCal even though he broke my heart.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469025352ra/19772500.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, I really loved loved loved what happened the middle of the book until the end! It was amazing.. <b>BUT</b> the beginning was so <b>BORINGGGGGG</b>!! Yess, I said it!! <br/>------------------------------------------------<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501927455i/23511022._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>------------------------------------------------<br/>King's Cage was lot o</span>
  <span id="freeText7624256031939621521" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You aren’t alone.” The hope in his eyes cuts deeply. “You have your crown.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439246972ra/15813352.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why???? That ending killed me!!!! Now I see it! Now I feel it! <i>Anyone can betray anyone</i>!<br>I'm still #teamCal even though he broke my heart.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469025352ra/19772500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I really loved loved loved what happened the middle of the book until the end! It was amazing.. <b>BUT</b> the beginning was so <b>BORINGGGGGG</b>!! Yess, I said it!! <br>------------------------------------------------<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501927455i/23511022._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>------------------------------------------------<br>King's Cage was lot of surprises:<br>1) I don't still hate Maven! I was angry because of what he did! I just feel sorry for him. Elara took his love for his brother and father when he was a child and she tried to take his love for Mare but he said it didn't work! I don't think he loves her anymore. I think he did but Elara took his love for her and it became an obsession. Cal wants to find someone who will be able to fix him. Even if they fix him, I don't think that would be redeemed for what he did.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1490018862ra/22273269.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2)I never thought I would say that but I really liked Evangeline!! I will admit that I hated her in the first book but now I understand her. I admire her loyalty to her parents and brother even though it's against her free will and who she wants to be with. It's really sad that Evangeline, Elaine and Ptolemus have a strange agreement! I hope she end up with who she wants!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455921821ra/18168879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3)Mare was less annoying, thank God! Mare FINALLY admits her love for Cal and Cal for her! And life was good... so so good.... until that Cal's grandmother(that bitch) had a plan to Cal become a King! Her plan worked and she fucked us up!!!<br>Cal accepts it!<br>Cal didn't choose Mare!<br>Mare didn't choose Cal!<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I thought I knew what heartbreak was. I thought that was what Maven did to me. When he stood and left me kneeling. When he told me everything I ever thought him to be was a lie. But then, I believed I loved him.<br>I know now, I didn't know what love was. Or what even the echo of heartbreak felt like.<br>To stand in front of a person who is your whole world and be told you are not enough. You are not the choice. You are a shadow to the person who is your sun.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471807179ra/20109627.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4) I don't have anything to say about Cameron even though she had her own POV!<br>Oww, I have something. Bravo for saving her brother... that's it. I think Kilorn and Cameron would do a good couple. I don't have to say much about him either :P<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454180664ra/17928537.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5)I was so right about Farley's pregnancy!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459100499ra/18570136.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Anyway, I admire Farley. She is so strong even though she feels so much pain. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492035293ra/22475786.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>

  <span id="freeText8856368625853320575" style="display:none"><u>3.5 All Will Burn ★'s</u> <br><br><i>“Now I'm in a king's cage. But so is he. My chains are Silent Stone. His is the crown.”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527657667ra/25618635.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I thought I knew what heartbreak was. I thought that was what Maven did to me. When he stood and left me kneeling. When he told me everything I ever thought him to be was a lie. But then, I believed I loved him.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406622686i/10574845._SX540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <b>Small spoilers may insue</b><br><br>DAMN, 'King's Cage' gave me so many feels! And that ending for reals broke my heart 😭😭. Damn you Cal, damn youuuuuu!!!!! Damn the crown, damn it all to the hells! <br><br>Though I did like this book, I gotta say it has to be my least favorite in this series thus far. I guess I was expecting a lot more with Mare's imprisonment and her being King Maven's puppet. Maven, the guy she once loved. Mare was basically left in a room, a room with great accommodations mind you. Sure there was that (ONE) time when she was mentally tortured by a Whisper. Yeah okay, it was pretty freaking bad and I really felt for her!! And being handcuffed with silent stone to suppress her lightning ability that left her feeling a deep sense of loss because she couldn't touch her power... Mare is powerless without her lightning. But still, I would have like a bit more torture or something! Other than Mare's pride being broken and being paraded around for all the world to see it could have been a hells of a lot worse! I'm giving it a 3.5 star because I know it could have so much better :D Victoria Aveyard writing was done very nicely, I just really don't care for Cameron's POV. I am <b>NOT</b> a big fan of her's, all she does is shit talk ♥Cal♥! I really like the plot of these books, the world is well thought out and the characters are pretty fantastic, minus a couple of them lol! Sure, Mare is a bit self-righteous at times and annoying at others but it wouldn't be <i>Red Queen</i> without her :) Even though the ending mad me upset with Cal and his decision, he's sill, my man! I love Cal so very much but its true he really can't make up his own mind and instead, he does as others expect of him. Okay well, I'm gonna keep this one short because I can't wait another minute to start the final book in this series <i>War Storm</i>!!! <br><br><b>#teamCal Forever!!</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406622686i/10574845._SX540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><i>“To stand in front of a person who is your whole world and be told you are not enough. <div id="review_1553384335" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1553384335" />
    <a title="Coreen ❇" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43075248-coreen"><img alt="Coreen ❇" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604385336p2/43075248.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1553384335?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Coreen ❇" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Coreen ❇" href="/user/show/43075248-coreen">Coreen ❇</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1553384335" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17141565710767827485"><b>I AM DEAD INSIDE. THIS BOOK FUCKING SHATTERED ME. I AM NOT BREATHING. I AM COMPLETELY DESTROYED. I AM SO FUCKING DONE.</b><br/><br/>---<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Samos, Calore, Cygnet. The Rift, Norta, the Lakelands. All driven by greed, all ready to break one another for an already broken crown."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Why do authors insist on torturing their readers? I mean, there's the ending to the Crystal Storm and now this. Why shatter my heart into two and make me wait for another year to piece it back together? Why Victoria Aveyard? Why M</span>
  <span id="freeText17141565710767827485" style="display:none"><b>I AM DEAD INSIDE. THIS BOOK FUCKING SHATTERED ME. I AM NOT BREATHING. I AM COMPLETELY DESTROYED. I AM SO FUCKING DONE.</b><br><br>---<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Samos, Calore, Cygnet. The Rift, Norta, the Lakelands. All driven by greed, all ready to break one another for an already broken crown."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Why do authors insist on torturing their readers? I mean, there's the ending to the Crystal Storm and now this. Why shatter my heart into two and make me wait for another year to piece it back together? Why Victoria Aveyard? Why Morgan Rhodes? Why Rick Riordan? WHYYYYYYYYY?!<br><i>I still love the torture, so no regrets. Lol</i><br><br>After being stuck with the paranormal romance world —which was kinda bleak compared to the YA fantasy world— I was left craving for a genre like this.<br><br>Victoria Aveyard's writing style never changed. It was still captivating and impossible to put down once you started reading it.<br>The <i>character development</i> of Mare, Maven and Cal was outstanding. They all learned from their past mistakes and changed for the better... or worse.<br><br><i>Mare</i>, her growth as a character was so shocking (See the connection? Lightning girl = shocking. Lol I made myself laugh). From a whiny broken girl she evolved into a cunning and strong willed woman. She refused to believe what she sees and was constantly suspicious about everything.<br><br><i>Cal</i>, I saw only a few glimpses of this broken prince in this book but it was enough to build my love for his character. I mean, aside from the fact that he is smoking hot (that's a pun again) he refused to give up his love for his younger brother. Despite the torture that Maven did to Mare, the deception and the betrayal. He still believes that his brother can change. Not that I can blame him, I love Maven too.<br><br><i>Maven</i>, there's just something broken about him that I wanted to fix and I think that's the reason why people adore Calore. Things about his personality became more crystal clear in this novel. I used to love him more than Cal but I'm afraid I love Cal more than him now, but no need to worry I still love him all the same. Lol<br><br>Everything about this book was great, the world building, the characters, the battle, the romance. It all screams perfection and I couldn't agree more to it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1482923469p8/1793410.jpg" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17141565710767827485" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1823922292" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1823922292" />
    <a title="Ahmed  Ejaz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53694260-ahmed-ejaz"><img alt="Ahmed  Ejaz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598778737p2/53694260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1823922292?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ahmed  Ejaz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ahmed  Ejaz" href="/user/show/53694260-ahmed-ejaz">Ahmed  Ejaz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53694260-ahmed-ejaz?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53694260-ahmed-ejaz?shelf=full-lengths">full-lengths</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1823922292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10938089172894177656">☆☆2.5 Stars☆☆<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Power seduces all, and it makes us blind. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote>This book was my most wanted book. I wanted to read this book more than anything. Anything!! When I got my hands on this, I was kind of...repenting. Repenting on what I was wanting. <br/>First of all, this book's beginning was different from Glass Sword's which was kind of very slow. Beginning of this book was looking breath-taking. I thought I would get more than I wanted. But this book couldn't be able to give what I even expected.</span>
  <span id="freeText10938089172894177656" style="display:none">☆☆2.5 Stars☆☆<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Power seduces all, and it makes us blind. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote>This book was my most wanted book. I wanted to read this book more than anything. Anything!! When I got my hands on this, I was kind of...repenting. Repenting on what I was wanting. <br />First of all, this book's beginning was different from Glass Sword's which was kind of very slow. Beginning of this book was looking breath-taking. I thought I would get more than I wanted. But this book couldn't be able to give what I even expected. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>OVERVIEW</u>
</b><br />Book begins exactly where the last book ended. Mare is on the edge of death (apparently) but rather than killing her, Maven sets her for a propaganda. He sets her for every bad deed he will be going to commit. <br />The main development in this book is HISTORY. We get to know more about the world, how it came into existence, how the discrimination of the world was made, how the war was first started and for what etc...<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />This book has completely changed what I was thinking. I thought this book would have more on war between Lakeland and Norta. But I was completely wrong. That war just ended in two to three lines. <br />Now Lakeland is the ally of Norta against the rebellion which is led by the Grandmother of Cal, the rightful heir to the throne.<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <b>THINGS I DIDN'T LIKE</b>
</u><br />=&gt; When I saw Maven didn't kill Mare, I was shocked. Then I thought 'Maven couldn't be that kind. Oh! He is Elara's son after all. He will must make her suffer more than she deserves'. But NO. Her punishment was only to wear manacles made of silent stone. With manacles, she was allowed to live like a princess.<br /><br />=&gt; This book is the most boring book I have ever read. Really! Except for 4 to 5 chapters, this book is a total junk. Useless! Just to waste pages (by which most of the trees could have been saved..lol) and to fill the so-called 3rd book in the series of 4 books. I am not quite understanding this! What is the point in making the series of 4 books? 3 or 2 sounds a lot better for this type of story.<br /><br />=&gt; Mare, I am beginning to hate her more. The more I was reading her, the more I found myself hating her. She always thinks that everyone is trying to kill her. Her thinking is soo over! Kind of exaggerated. Or at one moment she is willing to be killed and another she is afraid of being killed. She is such a confusion. At least for me.<br /><br />=&gt; Whenever there is the name of Maven, there must be the name of her mother. Like I don't know Maven is Elara's son. Why there is a need of constant reminder!<br /><br />=&gt; Cameron, she is more insufferable than Mare. Her POV is a true torture for me. Her POV is supposed to show us the proceedings of Scarlet Guard as Mare is in Maven's so-called Cage. That's okay and I completely understand it. But when this book tells her background, that's not okay for me. Why would I want to know that. She isn't even one of main characters. She is just a filler. This thing just helps in making the book more insufferable. <br /><br />=&gt; I didn't like how this book has changed Evengeline. Well, I couldn't get the point in doing so. That could have been different. <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />=&gt; Cal, why the heck he has chaged in the ending. Oh sorry! I forgot! This book was warning me. But I wasn't expecting him actually doing it. <br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><u>
  <b>THINGS I LIKED</b>
</u> <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />=&gt; Interrogation of Mare by Samson, that was kind of replay of the previous books. I liked that.<br /><br />=&gt; History of the world<br /><br />=&gt; Death scene of Samson, the fight of Samson with Cal and Mare was excellently written.<br /><br />=&gt; Cal rescuing Mare with Scarlet Guard, that was my favourite portion of the entire novel. <br /><br />=&gt; 2nd last chapter, which was from Evengeline's POV. That was a short conclusion of almost of the novel.<br /><br />=&gt; Maven, sometimes I liked him, sometimes I didn't. But overall, he is...fine. Little better than everyone else.<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I am quite disappointed right now. But equally curious about the last novel. Really hope for a good conclusion. :(<br /><br /><b> <i> All will burn </i></b>[cover says]<br /><i> And All has burned </i><br />Don't let this happen to the next one. Please, Mrs. Aveyard!<br /><br />March 1, 2017</span>
  <a data-text-id="10938089172894177656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2338977504" />
    <a title="Charlotte May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14002983-charlotte-may"><img alt="Charlotte May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596906925p2/14002983.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2338977504?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Charlotte May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Charlotte May" href="/user/show/14002983-charlotte-may">Charlotte May</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781409151197" href="/book/show/31323287-king-s-cage">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=sisters">sisters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=500-page-plus">500-page-plus</a>,

<span id="freeTextContainer16051676006147442774"><i> “Now I’m in a King’s cage. But so is he. My chains are silent stone. His is the crown.” </i><br/><br/>I’m having a real dilemma with this series. On the one hand, it’s easy to read, there are a lot of great characters and an exciting plot. <br/><br/>On the other hand, Mare is still pretty insufferable. She spent 6 months in Maven’s palace Whitefire, being tortured within an inch of her life and paraded around as a pet the rest of the time. This was a good plot device. However, Mare soon began repeating herself on a re</span>
  <span id="freeText16051676006147442774" style="display:none"><i> “Now I’m in a King’s cage. But so is he. My chains are silent stone. His is the crown.” </i><br /><br />I’m having a real dilemma with this series. On the one hand, it’s easy to read, there are a lot of great characters and an exciting plot. <br /><br />On the other hand, Mare is still pretty insufferable. She spent 6 months in Maven’s palace Whitefire, being tortured within an inch of her life and paraded around as a pet the rest of the time. This was a good plot device. However, Mare soon began repeating herself on a regular basis ‘I want to kill Maven” “I wish I could kill Maven” etc. Etc. While her point was valid, I knew how she felt the first time, it didn’t need repeating every couple of pages!<br />The second half of the book was just as bad. Having escaped her prison all she would do is remind us of the prison she escaped. Like yes I know this - I read 150 pages about it!<br /><br />I liked the chapters from Cameron’s POV - she was great and super relatable. I also appreciated the few chapters from Evangeline’s POV they were really interesting to see all the inter house politics. <br /><br />But overall, I can’t get used to Mare. She is vastly irritating. Unfortunately after this ending I still need to read the last one to see how it will all end, because I need to know! But I’m not sure how much I’ll enjoy it - my patience with this series is wearing thin.</span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1105063640" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1105063640" />
    <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines"><img alt="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466111136p2/30004027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1105063640?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines">Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1105063640" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5927064336631115181"><blockquote>
  <i>“She was his hurricane, and every nudge pulled him deeper into the eye of the storm.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>This book almost bored me to tears</b>. I can’t even count the number of time I actually fell asleep while reading it. It took me a full month to read it, one full month <b>feeling underwhelmed</b>, the worst part being concentrated on the first excruciating 60% or so. I don’t get why Victoria Aveyard spent so much time writing about the same thing over and over: <b>Mare being chained and miserable, Mare seeing Maven, awk</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5927064336631115181" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“She was his hurricane, and every nudge pulled him deeper into the eye of the storm.”</i>
</blockquote><br><b>This book almost bored me to tears</b>. I can’t even count the number of time I actually fell asleep while reading it. It took me a full month to read it, one full month <b>feeling underwhelmed</b>, the worst part being concentrated on the first excruciating 60% or so. I don’t get why Victoria Aveyard spent so much time writing about the same thing over and over: <b>Mare being chained and miserable, Mare seeing Maven, awkward conversations, Mare back to her cell/chamber, Mare angry breaking plates and throwing food. Repeat. </b> Was it supposed to show that she spent a lot of time as Maven prisoner? Was it supposed to make us understand that this was a kind of unhealthy routine? For all I know, it made Mare look like a childish person throwing tantrums around, and I couldn’t even feel the strength to pity her. <br><br>I knew beforehand that this book would contain more Maven than Cal, but still, I felt ready. But I wasn’t prepared how boring that would be. Because <b>there is so much emotionally-broken-Maven I can bear. </b> And the fact that I still resent him for his betrayal in Red Queen has nothing to do with why I disliked this book. I feel that during the first half of this book, we haven’t learned anything new from him. Yes, we know it is not his fault, that he is not truly a monster but that he was <i>made</i> and raised that way by his mother. But here it’s just confusing. We can see that Maven is not supposed to be a love interest anymore, at least not to Mare who made it clear to herself that his love is poisonous, but <b>she somehow kept some is misplaced empathy for him and felt so fake</b> I couldn’t feel anything except wondering what was wrong with her. In the end, Maven ended up being a flat villain and what he used to bring to the story is now gone.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“You are only a shadow, and who looks at shadows when they have flame?”</i>
</blockquote><br>I think that Cameron POV was part of what made this book even harder to like. I enjoyed her in Glass Sword, I liked her power and her rebellious mind, but here she became another brat. Her only purpose was to make us see some of what happened with the Scarlet Guard. But Cameron doubts and mood were really annoying; and in the end, anyone else could have been the Scarlet Guard POV. It could have become way more interesting with <b>Cal willing to lose everything to get Mare back, or Kilorn with his key role to make Silver, New Blood and Red less suspicious and more trusting around each other, or Farley coping with Shade death, becoming General and made a Guard Ranking Officer with Command of the Scarlet Guard while pregnant</b>. See, plenty of ideas here. Cameron doubts and mood were just annoying.<br><br>On the other way, I enjoyed a lot reading from Evangeline Samos’s POV. She was really mysterious to me in the previous books and I liked to learn that she is a grey character as well. I <b>loved her relationship with Elain, seeing her in her intimacy made her look softer and more human. </b> I understand her more now. She is still a badass fighter but she has weaknesses and a mind of her own. She was less ambitious than what it first seemed and I’m really looking forward to read more about her in the next instalment, I’m pretty sure that she can be the turning point for what is next to come.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“To stand in front of a person who is your whole world and be told you are not enough. You are not the choice. You are a shadow to the person who is your sun.” </i>
</blockquote><br>Last but not least, there is Cal. I loved him so bad. The fact that <b>he still hopes for Maven to redeem</b> is crushing my inside, it also makes him human, because he remembers when they were younger, he has a memory of who Maven used to be and who he could be if the damage made by his mother could be unmade. I melted over his love declaration(s) for Mare. He finally embraces how he feels about her and that was so sweet to witness. I’m not sure their relationship is really healthy and <b>I keep thinking that Mare is not good enough for him, but I want him to be happy, so if he wants Mare, then Mare it needs to be</b>. The epilogue was really the only part of the book where I actually had some tiny bit of feelings while reading. I was kind of off-track with how Victoria Aveyard decided to cut short the battle scene, but this scene touched me. Hell, it even broke my heart. I don’t know <b>whose pain hurt me the most. </b> Probably Cal’s, even though they both could have made a different choice. They both had the choice, and they both decided to follow their ambition instead of their heart. <b>In the end, both of them were wrong and right at the same time. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488810491i/22155310.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To wrap up, in my opinion, this book deserved no more than 1 star, but the second half, Evangeline POV, as well as the epilogue, saved my mood. Thanks to those, I’m decided to read the fourth and last book of this series once it comes out.<br><br><br>____________________________<br><u>
  <b>Pre-review</b>
</u><br>I can't believe how long it took me to read this book.<br>I can't believe how much I disliked it. <br>I can't believe it still managed to leave me heartbroken.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5927064336631115181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qwRR/QTYDYy8ALc0UYvg48n8yyh8hlcBvNYpOdymfIg6g/bZISjJoT1It+FvLH5o3imYZGCs0WOP7Jm8yaxg4g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AggihoyfCyY6sCAQ1qRJ+sWd+PO7AKHtgIC/MKkVt7uTj4WiqW/PC7v4IMXoA9dx0kirv6cqJ4+zug+1vB+r0Q==')})
  }
